# Translation file for QueueMetrics - en_US

- The name WombatDialer is a product and should be left unaltered. 
- The acronym "CSV" should be unaltered.
- The acronym "AMO" stands for Assisted Manual Outbound


## Language pack

General information about this language pack. The language name should be written in the
language itself, and will appear in the drop-down language selector.

    00-LanguageName=አማርኛ
    
Do not change the items below:

    dateformat_complete=dd MMMM yyyy, HH:mm
    dateformat_completeshort=dd/MM - HH:mm:ss
    dateformat_date=yyyy-MM-dd
    dateformat_flow=1
    dateformat_time=HH:mm:ss
    dateformat_timeshort=HH:mm

## AOUT


    # 👽 aout_act_billable -> Billable activities
    aout_act_billable=?የሚከፈልባቸው እንቅስቃሴዎች
    # 👽 aout_act_notbillable -> Non billable activities
    aout_act_notbillable=?የማይከፈልባቸው እንቅስቃሴዎች

    aout_activity=?እንቅስቃሴ
    # 👽 aout_agent -> Agent name

    aout_agent_report=?ዝርዝር የወኪል ሪፖርት
    # 👽 aout_available_s -> Avail.
    aout_available_s=?ይገኛል።
    # 👽 aout_available_time -> Total agent available time:
    aout_available_time=?ጠቅላላ የወኪል የሚገኝበት ጊዜ፡
    # 👽 aout_avg_sec -> Avg.
    aout_avg_sec=?አማካይ
    # 👽 aout_avg_talk_time -> Avg. Talk
    aout_avg_talk_time=?አማካይ ወሬ
    # 👽 aout_avg_wait_time -> Avg. Wait
    aout_avg_wait_time=?አማካይ መጠበቂያ

    # 👽 aout_call_res_by_feature -> Call results, by feature code

    # 👽 aout_call_res_by_outcome -> Call results, by outcomes

## Editor of security keys

Description of security keys:

    # 👽 keydesc_agaw -> User can access AGAW facades (for agents).
    keydesc_agaw=?ተጠቃሚ AGAW facades (ለወኪሎች) መድረስ ይችላል።
    # 👽 keydesc_agaw_adm -> User can access the AGAW administration screens
    keydesc_agaw_adm=?ተጠቃሚ AGAW አስተዳደር ስክሪኖችን መድረስ ይችላል።
    # 👽 keydesc_agaw_rep -> User can access the AGAW supervisor screen
    keydesc_agaw_rep=?ተጠቃሚ የ AGAW የበላይ ተቆጣጣሪን መመልከት ይችላል።
    # 👽 keydesc_agent -> User is an agent and sees agent page
    keydesc_agent=?ተጠቃሚ ወኪል ነው እና የወኪል ገጽን ይመለከታል።
    # 👽 keydesc_agrep -> User can filter reports by agent
    keydesc_agrep=?ተጠቃሚ በወኪል ሪፖርቶችን ማጣራት ይችላል።
    # 👽 keydesc_autoanswer_phone -> User can toggle Auto Answer on the softphone
    keydesc_autoanswer_phone=?ተጠቃሚ በሶፍትፎን ላይ ራስ-ሰር መልስ መቀያየር ይችላል
    # 👽 keydesc_batch_add -> Can add calls to an open batch
    keydesc_batch_add=?ጥሪዎችን ወደ ክፍት ስብስብ ማከል ይችላል።
    # 👽 keydesc_batch_adm -> Creates and closes batches for exporting audio
    keydesc_batch_adm=?ለድምጽ ወደ ውጭ ለመላክ ስብስቦችን ይፈጥራል እና ይዘጋል
    # 👽 keydesc_batch_del -> Can remove calls from a batch.
    keydesc_batch_del=?ጥሪዎችን ከስብስብ ማስወገድ ይችላል።
    # 👽 keydesc_batch_view -> User can see audio export batches
    keydesc_batch_view=?ተጠቃሚ የድምጽ ወደ ውጭ መላኪያ ስብስቦችን ማየት ይችላል

## System configuration

### Editors of System properties

These apply to both "Edit configuration properties" and "Explore parameters":

    # 👽 cfgprops_title -> Edit QueueMetrics system parameters
    cfgprops_title=?የQueueMetrics የስርዓት መለኪያዎችን ያርትዑ
    # 👽 cfgprops_title_wizard -> Explore QueueMetrics system parameters
    cfgprops_title_wizard=?የQueueMetrics የስርዓት መለኪያዎችን ያስሱ
    # 👽 cfgprops_notice -> After saving, you need to log off and on again for the parameters to be loaded.
    cfgprops_notice=?ካስቀመጡ በኋላ፣ መለኪያዎቹ እንዲጫኑ መውጣትና እንደገና መግባት ያስፈልግዎታል።
    # 👽 cfgprops_n_items -> N. Properties found
    cfgprops_n_items=?N. ንብረቶች ተገኝተዋል
    # 👽 cfgprops_input -> Enter one or more properties to set, one per line
    cfgprops_input=?ለማዘጋጀት አንድ ወይም ከዚያ በላይ ንብረቶችን ያስገቡ፣ በአንድ መስመር አንድ
    # 👽 cfgprops_comment -> Reason for this change
    cfgprops_comment=?የዚህ ለውጥ ምክንያት
    # 👽 cfgprops_sort_by -> Sort by
    cfgprops_sort_by=?በዚህ ደርድር
    # 👽 cfgprops_sort_bydate -> Last update
    cfgprops_sort_bydate=?የመጨረሻ ዝማኔ
    # 👽 cfgprops_sort_byname -> Name
    cfgprops_sort_byname=?ስም
    # 👽 cfgprops_col_name -> Property name
    cfgprops_col_name=?የንብረት ስም
    # 👽 cfgprops_col_value -> Current value
    cfgprops_col_value=?የአሁኑ እሴት
    # 👽 cfgprops_col_comment -> Reason
    cfgprops_col_comment=?ምክንያት
    # 👽 cfgprops_history_date -> Date
    cfgprops_history_date=?ቀን
    # 👽 cfgprops_history_user -> User
    cfgprops_history_user=?ተጠቃሚ
    # 👽 cfgprops_history_value -> Value
    cfgprops_history_value=?እሴት
    # 👽 cfgprops_history_previous -> Previous entries
    cfgprops_history_previous=?የቀድሞ ግቤቶች
    

These are obsolete:

    # 👽 cfgprops_file_saved -> File configuration.properties saved at
    cfgprops_file_saved=?ፋይል configuration.properties በዚህ ላይ ተቀምጧል
    # 👽 cfgprops_ioerror -> I/O error on file configuration.properties - check server logs.
    cfgprops_ioerror=?በፋይል configuration.properties ላይ I/O ስህተት - የአገልጋይ ምዝግብ ማስታወሻዎችን ይመልከቱ።
    # 👽 cfgprops_nocontent -> File not saved: for your safety, the file cannot be empty or contain HTML tags.
    cfgprops_nocontent=?ፋይል አልተቀመጠም፦ ለደህንነትዎ ሲባል ፋይሉ ባዶ መሆን ወይም HTML መለያዎችን መያዝ የለበትም።
    # 👽 cfgprops_not_editable -> The configuration.properties cannot be edited.
    cfgprops_not_editable=?configuration.properties ሊስተካከል አይችልም።
    # 👽 cfgprops_wrong_line -> File not saved - Wrong format for line
    cfgprops_wrong_line=?ፋይል አልተቀመጠም - ለመስመሩ የተሳሳተ ቅርጸት
